Deck Lists: Top Block Constructed Decks
=======================================



 Posted in **Event Coverage**
 on June 11, 2011 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/authorpic_EventCoverageStaff.jpg)
By Event Coverage Staff










Listed below are the deck lists from Pro Tour Nagoya which finished with 18 or more points in the 10 rounds of Block Constructed play.

#####
